  var QueryString = function QueryString() {
    var vars = {};
    window.location.href.replace(/[?&]+([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function (m, key, value) {

  };

  var getPage = function getPage(globalTrackingObj) {
    switch (globalTrackingObj.pageLayout) {
      case 'NotFoundPage':
        return 'Page Not Found';

      case 'LeafPage':
        if (globalTrackingObj.siteSection !== 'Member Center') {

    }

  window.track = function(){var globalTracking = window.bg.globalTracking; var user = window.bg.user;globalTracking.pageLayout = 'HomePage';globalTracking.pageUrl = window.location.href;globalTracking.trackEvent = function trackEvent(props) {

    var QueryString = function QueryString() {
      var vars = {};
      window.location.href.replace(/[?&]+([^=&]+)=([^&]*)/gi, function (m, key, value) {
        vars[key] = value;
      });
      return vars;
    };

    var queryParams = QueryString();
    /* eslint-disable */

    var formattedLeafString = function formattedLeafString(globalTrackingObj) {
      return globalTrackingObj.storyThread.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase() + globalTrackingObj.storyThread.substring(1);
    };

    var getPage = function getPage(globalTrackingObj) {
      switch (globalTrackingObj.pageLayout) {
        case 'LeafPage':
          return "".concat(globalTrackingObj.siteSection, " | ").concat(formattedLeafString(globalTrackingObj), " | ").concat(globalTrackingObj.articleHeadline);

        default:
          return globalTracking.page;
      }
    };

    var getProp4 = function getProp4(globalTrackingObj) {
      switch (globalTrackingObj.pageLayout) {
        case 'HomePage':
          return undefined;

        case 'TagPage':
          return 'Automated';

        case 'LeafPage':
          return "".concat(formattedLeafString(globalTrackingObj), " Page: LeafPage");

        default:
          return globalTrackingObj.pageLayout;
      }
    };

    var getProp6 = function getProp6(globalTrackingObj) {
      switch (globalTrackingObj.pageLayout) {
        case 'HomePage':
          return 'homepage';

        case 'LeafPage':

          return globalTrackingObj.pageOrAssetType;
      }
    };

   window.sophiWallHitEvent = function(wallType){
      window.sophi.sendEvent({
        "type": "wall_hit",
        "data": {
            "type": wallType,
            "name": "regular" //string, internal wall name
        }
      });

    window.sophiTag = function(){
      window.sophi=window.sophi||{};
      window.sophi.q=window.sophi.q||[];window.sophi.sendEvent=function(a){window.sophi.q.push(a)};
      window.sophi.data = window.sophi.data || {
        "page": {
          "type": "section",
          "breadcrumb": "homepage",
          "sectionName": "homepage",
          "title": window.bg.globalTracking.articleHeadline,
          "datePublished": window.bg.globalTracking.publishDate
        },
        "visitor": {
          "type": window.meterObject && window.meterObject.userInfo ? "Subscribed" : "Anonymous",
          "isLoggedIn": window.meterObject && window.meterObject.userInfo && window.meterObject.userInfo.authenticated ? true : false,
          "uid": window.bg.globalTracking.registrationID
        },
        "environment": {
          "version": window.bg.globalTracking.cms + " " + window.bg.globalTracking.codeVersion,
          "environment": window.bg.globalTracking.environmentTier === "Live" ?
            "prod": window.bg.globalTracking.environmentTier === "QA" ? "stg" : "dev",
        },
        "content": {
          "type": "article",
          "contentId": window.bg.globalTracking.articleID,
          "accessCategory": window.bg.page.exemptFromMeter ? "free access" : "metered views",
          "byline": [],
          "creditLine": "",
          "accessName": ""
        }
      };
      window.sophi.settings = window.sophi.settings || {
        "trackerName": "sophiTracker",
        "loadFrom": "https://cdn.sophi.io/latest/sophi.min.js",
        "client": "boston_globe",
        "linkedDomains": ["bostonglobe.com","boston.com","globe.com"]
      };
      try{eval('let id = Symbol("id"), a = [...new Set([0,1])].includes(0);');}catch(e){ window.sophi.settings.loadFrom = "https://cdn.sophi.io/latest/sophi.legacy.min.js";};(function(){if(!window[window.sophi.settings.trackerName]){var a=document.createElement("script");var b=document.getElementsByTagName("script")[0];a.async=1;a.src=window.sophi.settings.loadFrom;b.parentNode.insertBefore(a,b);}})();
      window.sophi.sendEvent({"type":"page_view"});
      if (window.meterObject && window.meterObject.meterState.paywall) {
        window.sophiWallHitEvent("paywall-metered");
      } else if (window.meterObject && window.meterObject.meterState.incognito) {
        window.sophiWallHitEvent("incognito-wall");
      }
    };
    if (window.meterObject && window.meterObject.meterState.result) {
      window.sophiTag();
    } else if (window.meterObject) {
      window.meterObject.observationController.addEventObserver("meterStateChange", window.sophiTag);
    }

           <a aria-label="A Beautiful Resistance" class="card color_inherit" href="/2020/10/28/metro/beautiful-resistance/">
            <h2 class="headline | bold border_box font_primary margin_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:14px">
             <span class="overline | bold border_box color_gray font_primary width_full inline_block margin_bottom_6 uppercase" style="background-color:auto;border:0px;border-color:auto;color:auto;font-size:10px;letter-spacing:.75px">
              Jeneé Osterheldt
             </span>
             <div class="image | margin_left_16 margin_bottom_10 width_full false false" id="">
              <figure class="font_primary margin_center false false" id="img-3d87631a-70e6-4a07-92b5-98dcb0728dab" style="height:auto">

             <span>
              A Beautiful Resistance
             </span>
             <div class="deck | border_box inline_block font_primary padding_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:12px;line-height:1.3">
              <div>
               Black joy, Black lives, as celebrated by culture columnist Jeneé Osterheldt.
               <!-- -->
              </div>
             </div>
            </h2>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="container | align_items_start inline_block col ws-12 desktop-12 tablet-12 width_full">
         <div class="s_c | align_items_start grid padding_horizontal width_full">
          <div class="card | inline_block img_r padding_null margin_top margin_left margin_right margin_bottom width_full i_o_h_d-hw" style="background-color:auto">
           <a aria-label="Boston Globe launches ‘Fresh Start’ initiative: People can apply to have past coverage about them reviewed " class="card color_inherit" href="/2021/01/22/metro/boston-globe-launches-fresh-start-initiative-people-can-apply-update-or-anonymize-coverage-them-thats-online/">
            <h2 class="headline | bold border_box font_primary margin_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:14px">
             <div class="image | margin_left_16 margin_bottom_10 width_full false false" id="">
              <figure class="font_primary margin_center false false" id="img-d06a93f8-e5d2-49c8-891f-ced9b23ad665" style="height:auto">
               <img alt="" class="height_a width_full width_full--mobile width_full--tablet-only" data-src="https://cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/bostonglobe/X2Y4XCCXKAI6PDFZ55TGZZKMXU.jpg" id="img-d06a93f8-e5d2-49c8-891f-ced9b23ad665-image" src="https://bostonglobe-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/fWmDVW0nGXQtgfdH3Xu0XOr7inA=/20x11/filters:focal(1045x10:1055x0)/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/bostonglobe/X2Y4XCCXKAI6PDFZ55TGZZKMXU.jpg"/>
               <figcaption class="img_caption | margin_horizontal_0--mobile margin_horizontal_0--tablet text_align_right">
                <span class="credit uppercase">
                </span>
               </figcaption>
              </figure>
             </div>
             <span>
              Boston Globe launches ‘Fresh Start’ initiative: People can apply to have past coverage about them reviewed
             </span>
             <div class="deck | border_box inline_block font_primary padding_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:12px;line-height:1.3">
              <div>
               Similar to “right to forget” programs that have cropped up across the country, the undertaking is meant to address the lasting impact that stories about past embarrassments, mistakes, or minor crimes, forever online, can have on a person’s life.
               <!-- -->
              </div>
             </div>
            </h2>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="container | align_items_start inline_block col ws-12 desktop-12 tablet-12 width_full">
         <div class="s_c | align_items_start grid padding_horizontal width_full">
          <div class="card | inline_block img_r padding_null margin_top margin_left margin_right margin_bottom width_full i_o_h_d-hw" style="background-color:auto">
           <a aria-label="Last Words: Is death the great equalizer?" class="card color_inherit" href="/2020/09/30/nation/last-words-is-death-great-equalizer/">
            <h2 class="headline | bold border_box font_primary margin_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:14px">
             <span class="overline | bold border_box color_gray font_primary width_full inline_block margin_bottom_6 uppercase" style="background-color:auto;border:0px;border-color:auto;color:auto;font-size:10px;letter-spacing:.75px">
              Globe Spotlight Investigation
             </span>
             <div class="image | margin_left_16 margin_bottom_10 width_full false false" id="">
              <figure class="font_primary margin_center false false" id="img-b5b3f2a3-11b8-4084-9df7-cfced00ef59f" style="height:auto">
               <img alt="" class="height_a width_full width_full--mobile width_full--tablet-only" data-src="https://cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/bostonglobe/ELZYDPHYA5HJ5CODVZFEN5UUHE.jpg" id="img-b5b3f2a3-11b8-4084-9df7-cfced00ef59f-image" src="https://bostonglobe-prod.cdn.arcpublishing.com/resizer/VUj414qzSmwvDfFjqyU-57-uuoY=/20x11/filters:focal(595x10:605x0)/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/bostonglobe/ELZYDPHYA5HJ5CODVZFEN5UUHE.jpg"/>
               <figcaption class="img_caption | margin_horizontal_0--mobile margin_horizontal_0--tablet text_align_right">
                <span class="credit uppercase">
                </span>
               </figcaption>
              </figure>
             </div>
             <span>
              Last Words: Is death the great equalizer?
             </span>
             <div class="deck | border_box inline_block font_primary padding_bottom" style="color:auto;font-size:12px;line-height:1.3">
              <div>
               Quite the contrary, a Spotlight investigation shows. Death exposes in high relief the layers of inequities, in race and income, care and opportunity, that shape life down to its final hours. It is a truth the pandemic has only underscored — one hard to see, because it is so much easier to look away.
               <!-- -->
              </div>
             </div>
            </h2>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>

            var getClosest = function (elem, selector) {
              for ( ; elem && elem !== document; elem = elem.parentNode ) {
                if ( elem.matches( selector ) ) return elem;
              }
              return null;
            };
            var footerSocialLinks = document.querySelectorAll('[data-footer-onclick]');

            for (var i = 0; i < footerSocialLinks.length; i++) {
              footerSocialLinks[i].addEventListener('click', function(event) {
                const footerSocialLink = getClosest(event.target, '[data-footer-onclick]');
                const social = footerSocialLink.getAttribute('data-footer-onclick');

                window.bg &&
                window.bg.globalTracking &&
                window.bg.globalTracking.trackEvent &&
